    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    registration_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE review (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    game_id INT,
    player_id INT,
    rating DECIMAL(2, 1),
    review_text TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES game(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES player(id)
);

CREATE TABLE game (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    release_date DATE,
    platform VARCHAR(100)

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><stat>update achievements set achievement_name = 'master of the game' where player_id = 3;</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE games (game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_name VARCHAR(255), game_genre VARCHAR(255), game_release_date DATE);
